The photographer is very dedicated and has a good photography level. In short, East Taihu Hotel is worth staying in again.

Second, the other staff are very enthusiastic, and the shuttle bus is always on call, which is very convenient. Almost everyone I meet smiles and says hello. But maybe the housekeeping girl is an intern? Things were done a bit confusingly, and there was an indescribable dullness in arranging extra beds and providing software services.
The hot springs are very comfortable to soak in. There are not many people and the environment is good. Although the hot spring pools are not as many as Wang Yan's, they are suitable for friends who like a private and customized feeling.
In addition, the double electric car is very interesting. You can drive around the lake to take photos and enjoy the lake view, and you can also drive it around the resort. Children especially like it.

The hot spring in the hotel is very comfortable, there are not many people, and the children like it very much. There is also a playground for feeding small animals and small children, and you can also do baking crafts. The restaurant for breakfast is not big, so it seems to be crowded. It is recommended to stagger the peak hours, otherwise you will queue up.
